> Can't cut a onion properly  > Also thinks she can develop a dish from scratch   Cooking as everything in life is about phases, you cannot walk if you are unable to crawl... This December I was with my sister, she was in charge of cutting potatoes really thinly for a millefeuille with bechamel, she couldn't cut them really thinly and asked me if she could do the bechamel instead, I replied "if you can't cook some potato thinly, how would you think you are ready to make a bechamel?". This anecdote applies here, learn the basics, meaning months and months even years of proper technique and knowledge of why and then maybe you can come up with something that it is balanced and flavourful not simply because you chose 3 ingredients and had to mix them together no matter what or because it was envision, which much of the time is just about obstinacy. It is the first time I see a video and I know why it was so hard for you to see the benefit of cooking since you must have taken double the time it took you for preparation just picking up the trash you left everywhere in the kitchen.... advice, pick up the trash you are leaving on the counter, it is a mess and dirty for the rest of the preparation. Collect, clean and tidy up things as you cook and finish using them.  Also second advice, boil the green peas, put them in cold water, blend them with a bit of their cooking water, basil, olive oil and some heavy cream for cooking, there you have a vibrant green, kind of soup.

Every now and then, I have days like today. My head is too heavy to lift from my pillow, and my eyes well-up before they've even opened. The sun obnoxiously takes space in my mind, and my alarm screams at me to get my shameful self up and go to class. I turned it off today, and I slept through my 8:00am lesson.   I know I'm just one in a billion and my story isn't exactly relevant. But, I finally decided to wipe my face and leave the house. Only because I knew I would feel so guilty if I stayed in bed all day with pitiful tears streaming down my cheeks, watching sad Tik-Toks. I drove myself to Starbucks and ordered my favorite drink, hoping it would help. I parked in an open parking-lot to watch the clouds, stirring my Macchiato... My passenger seat felt extra empty today. My best friend has recently drifted away without warning, and without anything to cause it. I've been feeling so lonely, and it feels like nothing matters without her. Class has been so hard to show up to, and music has suddenly grown this dull sound. I've been burnt-out before, but never because of this. If anything, I'm just so tired from the anxiety that my stupid anxious attachment style is enduring.   I know it's not your exact situation, and I don't relate completely, but I understand needing a break. It feels like you need to sleep for 10 years, and withdraw yourself from life periodically. And even then, it won't feel like enough and you'll wake up to the same exhausting feeling. And on top of all of that, having to mask your raw emotions for the people who look up to you, despite the permanent hot rock in your stomach, is the thing that will hurt more than any traumatic experience.   I listened to your podcast as the Sun carefully hid behind the horizon, and again, you've helped me through one of the hardest times of my life. You deserve someone who does the same for you. Your mental health and wellness matters so much more than a video, or a voice recording.   We love your videos and podcasts, of course, but we love YOU more.   Please, PLEASE... Choose peace, always. Only do what makes you happiest, and please don't ever feel like you need to explain. Here's some advice I wish I could take myself... You are in control, Emma. Not us, not YouTube, not your friends, not your family, YOU are in control.   We love you, and we understand inevitably. <3

QUICK TIP FROM A CULINARY STUDENT!!! When chopping most things I use a hair pick! Just a regular like 2 dollar pick. It is honestly a game-changer. It makes chopping super quick and you don't have to worry about cutting your fingers. Also lets not forget that you get super even knife cuts. I love using It when I am going to pickle things, I remember from a previous video you pickle carrots often. Also in culinary school we learn that being a great chef is all about how to control HEAT! I also used to struggle because I figured if the heat was on high then it would cook faster, but I have learned to be patient and that good things take time. I hope this message finds you and if it does I hope you try it out and make something DELICIOUS!! stay sweet :) <3

Here it is:   Have you ever had someone you wanted to be like? To embody and leave joy with everyone you interact with? My person is Emma. Emma has a lot of friends. She leaves an impact everywhere she goes. Emma is 20 years old. She was born on May 22nd, 2001. Emma is a Gemini!    Emma has a youtube channel with 11 million subscribers! You can call her famous! She started the youtube channel at 16! Emma spent an entire summer starting her channel, a video every day. By the end of the summer, she had grown her channel with a ton of videos and new subscribers! This is when I found her! This is when Emma really showed her love for photography and fashion. She would make videos with her friends going to take photos in front of the sunrise and bring outfits to showcase on her Instagram and online. They didnâ€™t only take sunrise photos, but they were clothing-focused.   Emma was a really good student while going to a private catholic all-girls school. Emma opens up about graduating early out of high school when youtube was doing amazing and starting to get profitable. Recently she has stated that the reason she did that, was because she was a good student. Emma had all her high school credits in 10th grade. The classes she was in were for college credits and preparedness.   After that emma really started to get big. She started making different content like cooking videos and vlogs with her mom and even other friends with channels.  They made videos together going places and making jokes. Emma has since distanced herself from them because they didn't treat her the best.   	Emma and her family go on a trip together every year. They go and visit Maine and her grandparents. This is where Emma had fun. Her grandmother set up an entire fake fan asking for a picture to make Emma happy. She was so surprised someone knew her from her channel. Emma was so ecstatic about this. She started taking it extra seriously because she had fans now!   Shortly after this Emma started looking for apartments in LA to live in. She found a cute loft apartment and moved in! Her mom is seen going through the apartment with her and helping her move in. After a few weeks, she went back home. Emma once again got two more friend groups after this that didn't exactly treat her well. Emma has opened up about their bullying and ill-words.  	Emma has her own coffee business, which is very successful. She sells cold brews and regular coffee beans. This is because early on you can see her affliction for coffee. Emma regularly makes coffee in her videos. Coffee is basically Emma's life force.   	Emma has a beautiful home. She knows how to decorate a house to feel like home. The way she makes money for this is through brand deals and her company. People who have employed her include, Louis Vuitton, Audible, and many others.	   Emma is really an outstanding woman. I hope to be like her one day, intelligent, funny, hard-working, and successful. Emma really has it all at her fingertips and has so much influence. I hope she sees how many of us look up to her.

Tips for anyone who never made a soup: smash the vegetables (not so much, just a bit) after you put them into the soup (if you cook them separate. You can cook them with the soup itself, it's the same, you save water and time). The soup gets creamy and the flavor from those vegetables is more present and you don't get so much floating food around. You also do not need to put the soup into a blender. If you're adding any leaf you don't have to cut it in order to give the soup their flavor, unless you really want to eat those so you cut it. Add the leaves, cut or not, when it's almost done like 2 minutes left and cook them with the soup for those left tiny minutes. It gets the same flavor and you don't have to lose cooking time nor time washing a blender.

Who is God in Islam ? Muslims believe that God has no partners or associates who share in His divinity or authority and that God is transcendent, unlike His creations, and thus has no physical form. Nor is God believed to exist in (or be represented by) any material object. A number of divine attributes or â€œnames,â€ which serve to describe God, are found in the Qurâ€™an. Some commonly known attributes include the Most Merciful, the Most Forgiving, the Most High, the Unique, and the Everlasting, among others.
Islam honors all the prophets who were sent to mankind. Muslims respect all prophets in general, but Jesus in particular, because he was one of the prophets who foretold the coming of Muhammad. EMMA , today I made the soup for a third time, paying attention to your heat cooking instruction, low , to low- medium. Had to supplement the fingerling potatoes with two other types, ( two by choice ) , both are of the smaller gourmet quality, spherical, 3/4 to 1 inch diameter, one style having red skin, the other had gold /yellow, both potatoe skins of a thin variety. I scrubbed them clean, cooked them with skins on for flavor enhancement , no slicing due to their size, ( bite sized pretty much), used 1 pound. On the English Peas that came in 6 ounce bags, fresh, I used two bags , 12 ounces, washed and picked out the cringed ones , a few unrecognizable pieces. Garlic, picked out 8 of the large peeled ones, medium chopped them. The shallots were 3 to a bag, chose two bags with medium to large sized shallots, removed the thin paper skin, and first layer of tough skin, all had a purple- ish color. Sliced length ways into halves, thin sliced half rounds, flat half down. Chopped 1/2 cup of fresh basil  without the heavy stems, medium / fine chop & pressed down a bit. Potatoes in a deeper sauce pan took 3 and 1/2 cups water to cover them. Used a pan cover, a low boil , 15 minute check skins were tender w/ centers done. At the ten minute point shallots & garlic went into the skillet of 3 tablespoons of olive oil, lid on pan , medium heat, softened in 5 minutes, but still partially firm. Added vegan boullion, 4 cubes, to potatoes , then 12 ounces of raw peas, and the onion w/ garlic and basil. Cooked 4 minutes on medium low w/ lid, once it was brought to a boil medium high. Or until peas are â€œâ€ just tender â€œâ€. You had mentioned over cooking things in the past,  I enjoyed this batch the most using tips you mention in making the soup. Definitely adopted , the soup is a meal tradition. Thank you Emma.

Hey, my tip for cooking good soup with any veggies you want:  1. Cut garlic and onions 2. Cut veggies you want,  (for example potatoes and carrots, since they have a similar hardness you can cut them into same sized pieces and have them cook together till they are done. If you choose other vegetables that donâ€™t have the thickness or hardness like a your other vegetables, you have to adjust it: either you cut them for example celery in the same size as the potatoes and put them in the pot a little after or you cut them a little bit bigger so that they can cook together with the rest. In the end itâ€™s all about your feeling, but you can always google how long the vegetable has to cook and so adjust it to your other vegetables. Anyways back to the recipe. 3. put oil in the cold pot, (never olive oil, itâ€™s not suited for cooking on high temperature only for salads. Use coconut oil, rapeseed oil, sunflower oil. You can even put a tiny bit of butter to the veggie oil for flavour but only butter may have the risk to get burnt easily.) 4. put garlic and onions in the cold oil and let them heat up together not too high not too low (in Germany I use a 6., if that may help anybody) 5. do not let them get brown or burnt! When they are shiny you can put your veggies in the pot and stir so that every veggie is covered in a bit oil. (The oil makes the veggies get hot on all surfaces and save the flavours) 6. After a few minutes you can put the water with any broth you want: you can use veggie broth from the supermarket, self made broth, chicken broth, there are many but for starters, zause veggie broth from the store and put it in the water. Donâ€™t forget to read on the package how much you need for your amount of water! 7. Now bring the water slowly to bubble, donâ€™t heat up to max right after you put the water bc it isnâ€™t boiling. It takes a bit and donâ€™t forget to cover with your lid! 8. Now be careful and donâ€™t let you water boil too hard, once it boils with the lid you can go down with the temperature slowly step by step. Once itâ€™s hot with the lid you will only need a small heat and it will cook perfectly. Set your timer for the food and always check on it!  8. Then you can season while it cooks with any spices you want. In the beginning simple is always the best and after you can try different recipes! 9. Always taste and adjust to your desire!  But the most important thing is to cook with all your live and heart. If you put love into the food, it WILL taste good, I promise!

Hear me out Emma. Peel the potatoes. Keeping the skin on is fine for frying, roasting and baking but not necessarily soups because it gives it an earthy flavour. Make more broth liquid this time and put the potatoes in the broth so it can absorb the flavour and the starch can thicken the broth. Take out potatoes 3/4 of the way done and put broth in blender. Add a couple of potatoes (and peas if you want) in the blender with the broth and then blend. This will give the broth more body. Add broth back into pot, add your almost done potatoes that you took out earlier, and add your peas and cook until peas and potatoes are done.

Emma did great with this recipe!! I'm from Brazil and we kinda have the soup she was looking for. Here we called it "caldo verde" (It could be "green soup"? idk lol) and the ingredients are potatoes, peas, kale, parsley, bacon and pepperoni sausage. It's really really good, we usually eat when the weather is cold. It's not considered fancy or anything, is more like a comfort food for cold days. If you'd like to try cooking at home, just search for "receita de caldo verde". Hope you enjoy it!!

Hey, I really enjoy cooking too. If you are looking forward to cooking more soups you should try pumpkin soup. You can make a spicy or sweet one. The basic recipe is: 1 sweat potato 1 hokkaido pumpkin  5 potatoes 3 onions pepper, salt  To make it sweat, you can add a mango or some banana. If you want to make it spicy you could add some garlic and ginger. Also different spices like chili powder or red pepper powder. To make the soup you basically chop all the things in small pieces. Then you take a soup pan and fry the chopped onions (with garlic and ginger if you want to use it). After the are golden brown you take the chopped potatoes and the chopped sweat potato and put them in the soup pan as well. After they got a little golden too you add the pumpkin (and the chopped mango if uou want. It should smell delicious. Then you keep frying till the pumpkin is just getting a little brown. You add 6-8 cups of water (so that all the vegetables are covered in water) and let it boil for at least 30 min. Add the pepper and salt (other spices if you want). If everything is getting soft you put it in the mixer and mix till smooth.  The pumpkin soup is ready!! Have great day
